## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="c18ef-1715">Windows Server 2008-Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c18ef-1715">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c18ef-1716">Diese Klasse enthält die folgenden Attribute für Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c18ef-1716">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>

## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="c18ef-2214">Windows Server 2008 R2-Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c18ef-2214">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c18ef-2215">Diese Klasse enthält die folgenden Attribute für Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c18ef-2215">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
